<script type="text/javascript" src="/kentico.resource/activities/kenticoactivitylogger/logger.js?pageIdentifier=5" async></script>

<script>
    function downloadPDF(e, publicId, hash) {
        e.preventDefault();

        const downloadUrl = window.location.origin + generateUrl(publicId, hash);
        window.open(downloadUrl);
    }

    function generateUrl(publicId, hash) {
        const baseUrl = '/pdf/downloadpdf';
        const type = 'External';

        const encodedPublicId = encodeURIComponent(publicId);
        const encodedHash = encodeURIComponent(hash);

        return `${baseUrl}?hash=${encodedHash}&targetPath=${encodedPublicId}&type=${type}`;
    }
</script>
